			Georiot.amazon.convertToGeoRiotLinks(153349, false);
		};
	  };
    });
  </script>

</head>

        const href = link.href;

        // --- SIMPLIFIED CONDITION ---
        // Check if the link's URL contains the word 'sandals' (case-insensitive is safer, but includes() is case-sensitive by default. Let's keep it simple as requested, assuming lower case 'sandals' in URLs)
        if (href && href.includes('sandals')) {

            // Attach a click listener only to links that match the condition
